$CATEGORY: $course$ / Examples / Switch_Cases1

::Switch Cases Level 1 #000::
What is the value of list after the switch/case block?
<pre>int list = 5;
switch (list) {
	case 6:
		list = 1;
		break;
	case 2:
		list = 0;
	case 3:
		list = 5;
		break;
	case 5:
		list = 3;
		break;
	case 0:
		list = 4;
		break;
	default:
		list = 6;
}</pre>
	{
	=3
	~8
	~2
	~5
	~6
	}

::Switch Cases Level 1 #001::
What is the value of bar after the switch/case block?
<pre>int bar = 5;
switch (bar) {
	case 0:
		bar = 4;
		break;
	case 5:
		bar = 2;
		break;
	case 2:
		bar = 0;
	case 1:
		bar = 3;
}</pre>
	{
	=2
	~1
	~4
	~5
	~3
	}

<pre>int standings = 5;
switch (standings) {
	case 2:

	case 3:
		standings = 1;
	case 5:
		standings = 4;
	case 1:
		standings = 0;
	default:
		standings = 3;
}</pre>
